***нора.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>нора́</a> (6983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nora</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>нора́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">norá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>норы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>но́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нора.html>нор</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hole, burrow, form <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">burrowed animal dwelling</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foxhole, dugout</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small, dark room; hole, diggings</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:норовить.html>норови́вший</a></b>

***нос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a> (433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nosъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*néh₂s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nos</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>носы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>носо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кровь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́са</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó krovʹ idjót iz <b>nósa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">His nose is bleeding.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bow, prow <i>(boats)</i></li>
<li>forepart, point</li>
<li>horn <i>(of an anvil)</i></li>
<li>headland, promontory, point <i>(geology)</i></li>
<li>lip <i>(for pouring)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сик</a> (9314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nósik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (little) nose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:носик.html>но́сик</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">child's speech</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma, u menjá <b>nósik</b> bolít.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mummy, my <b>nose</b> hurts.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bill, beak <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an insect or bird</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>spout <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a tube through which liquid is poured or discharged</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>face <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">forward part of some tools</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>си́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель</b>

Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:устройство.html>устро́йство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:носитель.html>носи́тель</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:носитель.html>носи́тели</a></i>).

***носить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a> (959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nositi</i>, iterative form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nesti</i> (whence also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:износить.html>износи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сносить.html>сноси́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry, to bear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by wind<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by water</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry along, to drive</li>
<li>to wear</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>Носи́ть</a></b> and its perfective counterparts, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:износить.html>износи́ть</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сносить.html>сноси́ть</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></b> are in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterpart, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></b>, is in the class of Russian concrete verbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***носиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a> (5278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nosítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rush, to rush around, to run/drive around (on a high speed)</li>
<li>to float around, to fly around</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fuss over, to pay too much attention to, to be obsessed with (an idea)</li>
<li>(of smells, sounds, etc.) to spread</li>
<li>to wear, to be worn (of clothes)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a></strong>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto plátʹje xorošó nosítʹsja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This dress wears well.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a></b> is an abstract verb. The counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is a concrete verb.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>си́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-нос-</b> |  суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b> |  глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> |  постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

***носовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́й</a> (29547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nosovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nose; nasal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровотечение.html>кровотече́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nosovóje</b> krovotečénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nose</b>bleed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nosovája</b> peredáča</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nose</b> gear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:платок.html>плато́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nosovój</b> platók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">handkerchief</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>nose</b> handkerchief</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проход.html>прохо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nosovój</b> proxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nasal</b> passage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prow, bow; forward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:носовой.html>носово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:украшение.html>украше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nosovóje</b> ukrašénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">figurehead <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a ship</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>prow</b> decoration</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***носок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носо́к</a> (2989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare etymology 2. Sense development is "little nose" -gt; "projection" -gt; "toe" -gt; "sock". Less likely from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nosók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надевать.html>надева́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носки́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nadevátʹ <b>noskí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on socks</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>toe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a boot, shoe or sock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>toe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a foot or hoof; especially the tip of the toe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">приподнима́ться <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носки́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pripodnimátʹsja na <b>noskí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rise on one's toes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>projection, nose <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a plane</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>таль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>че<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ский</b>

***нотация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ция</a> (23679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">notácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>homily, lecture, reprimand</li>
<li>notation</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ци<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>
